sapyrobileSi. sapyrobilis administracia mas axasiaTebs d


adebiTad da aRniSnavs, rom mas ar 


aqvs reJimis darRveva, keTilsindisierad asrulebs masve dakisrebul movaleobebs, karg

gamosworebis gzaze.

ebis administraciis mier gacemul daxasiaTebaSi


aRniSnulia, rom is aris mxatvari da sapyrobileSi eweva mravalmxriv mxatvrul

madlobebi. aris asociacia `firosmanis~ da asociacia `Semoqmedebis~ wevri. 1999w. aprils
